# Examples 与 Regression 映射

生成来源：`../warpx/Examples` 与 `../warpx/Regression/Checksum/benchmarks_json`。

- Example 输入/脚本条目数：657
- Regression benchmark JSON 条目数：356

## Examples

| 路径 | 初步主题 | 计划章节 | 验证用途 |
|---|---|---|---|
| `Examples/Physics_applications/beam_beam_collision/analysis_default_regression.py` | beam-beam collision / collider QED application | 96-100, 110, 125 | 本地 checksum helper；自动识别 plotfile/openPMD 并调用 `evaluate_checksum(...)`，为 beam-beam collider 场景提供历史输出基线，不增加独立 beamstrahlung / pair-yield 物理断言 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/beam_beam_collision/inputs_test_3d_beam_beam_collision` | beam-beam collision / collider QED application | 96-100, 105, 110, 125 | 3D beam-beam collider 骨架：两束 `125 GeV` 电子/正电子 Gaussian bunch 对撞，`do_electrostatic = relativistic` + collocated grid 求解自洽场，同时打开 Quantum Synchrotron、Breit-Wheeler、`ColliderRelevant` 与 `ParticleNumber` reduced diagnostics；当前是应用级 checksum baseline，不是解析 luminosity 强基准 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/beam_beam_collision/plot_fields.py` | beam-beam collision / collider QED application | 96-100, 110, 125 | openPMD 可视化 helper；按 `x/y` 切片展示 `|E|`、`|B|`、主束 `rho_beam*` 与次级对 `rho_ele*/rho_pos*` 的时序演化，不构成 regression 断言 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/beam_beam_collision/plot_reduced.py` | beam-beam collision / collider QED application | 96-100, 110, 125 | reduced-diagnostics 可视化 helper；从 `ColliderRelevant_beam1_beam2.txt` 与 `ParticleNumber.txt` 重建对撞时刻，并绘制每个 beam particle 的 photon 数与 NLBW pair 数时间曲线，不构成 regression 断言 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/capacitive_discharge/analysis_1d.py` | capacitive discharge / PIC-MCC / Turner benchmark | 92, 125 | 直接把 `ion_density_case_1.npy` 与内置 Turner case-1 参考离子密度 profile 做 `allclose`；重点验证 1D PICMI `background_mcc`、specialized external Poisson-solver callback，以及短步长 benchmark workflow 的联合合同 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/capacitive_discharge/analysis_default_regression.py` | capacitive discharge / PIC-MCC | 92, 125 | 通用 checksum helper；用于 2D native / PICMI capacitive-discharge 变体兜底，不提供独立放电物理断言 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/capacitive_discharge/analysis_dsmc.py` | capacitive discharge / PIC-MCC / DSMC / Turner benchmark | 92, 125 | 直接把 `ion_density_case_1.npy` 与另一组 case-1 参考离子密度 profile 做 `allclose`；重点验证 1D PICMI 骨架里 `background_mcc + DSMC` 双碰撞对象与同一 external Poisson solver callback 的接口一致性 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/capacitive_discharge/inputs_base_1d_picmi.py` | capacitive discharge / PIC-MCC / Turner benchmark | 92, 125 | 1D PICMI Turner-benchmark 骨架：可切换 `--pythonsolver` 与 `--dsmc`，统一覆盖 `background_mcc`、DSMC ionization、`callbacks.installpoissonsolver(...)` 外部泊松求解，以及 `ion_density_case_N.npy` 的最终 profile 导出 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/capacitive_discharge/inputs_test_2d_background_mcc` | capacitive discharge / PIC-MCC | 92, 125 | 2D native-input capacitive-discharge workflow baseline：He 背景气体、电子/离子 `background_mcc`、时变电极电势、lab-frame electrostatic 与 rho diagnostics；当前无独立 analysis，主要依赖 checksum 作为工作流级基线 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/capacitive_discharge/inputs_test_2d_background_mcc_picmi.py` | capacitive discharge / PIC-MCC | 92, 125 | 2D PICMI + pseudo-1D external Poisson-solver 版 workflow baseline：复现同一 He discharge 场景，并显式断言 callback solver 实际运行；当前无独立 analysis，主要依赖 checksum，重点覆盖 PICMI collision 接口与外部 solver 工作流 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/free_electron_laser/analysis_default_regression.py` | beam physics / free electron laser / boosted-frame diagnostics | 105, 125 | checksum helper；为 1D boosted-frame FEL 场景提供历史输出基线，不替代 `analysis_fel.py` 对 gain length 与 radiation wavelength 的强断言 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/free_electron_laser/analysis_fel.py` | beam physics / free electron laser / boosted-frame diagnostics | 105, 125 | 强分析：在 lab-frame 与 boosted-frame openPMD diagnostics 上分别拟合辐射 gain length，并用 FFT 反推出 radiation wavelength；重点验证 rigid beam + undulator external particle field + BTD 的联合合同 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/free_electron_laser/inputs_test_1d_fel` | beam physics / free electron laser / boosted-frame diagnostics | 105, 125 | 1D boosted-frame FEL 最小骨架：刚性注入 electron/positron 共流束抵消 space-charge，自发辐射由 `parse_B_ext_particle_function` 给出的 undulator `B_y(z)` 驱动，并同时写 boosted-frame 与 `BackTransformed` openPMD diagnostics |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/free_electron_laser/plot_sim.py` | free electron laser | 105, 125 | 可视化脚本；展示微聚束与辐射滑移，不构成 regression 断言 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/ion_beam_extraction/analysis_default_regression.py` | ion beam extraction | 105, 125 | 通用 checksum helper；自身不提供独立束流能量或电势断言 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/ion_beam_extraction/analysis_ion_beam_extraction.py` | ion beam extraction / electrostatic / embedded boundary | 105, 125 | 读取 `phi`、`eb_covered` 和 `Dplus` 粒子，要求抽出离子束尾部能量在 `40 keV` 目标附近的相对误差小于 `5%`；重点验证 `boundary.potential_* + warpx.eb_potential(x,y,z,t) + electrostatic solve + EB geometry` 的联合作用 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/ion_beam_extraction/inputs_test_3d_ion_beam_extraction` | ion beam extraction / electrostatic / embedded boundary | 105, 125 | 3D 电静离子束抽取场景；同时使用 `boundary.potential_lo_z` 与 `warpx.eb_potential(x,y,z,t)` 固定电极势，README 明确说明 `eb_potential` 只在 electrodes 上评估，电极间真空势分布仍由 Poisson 求解 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/laser_acceleration/analysis_1d_fluid_boosted.py` | fluid model | 101-104 | 对 1D boosted fluid WFA 场景的 `Ez/Jz/rho/Vz` 与理论 ODE 解做对照；laser 在这里是驱动器，不是单独的注入场断言对象 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/laser_acceleration/analysis_default_regression.py` | laser injection / LPI | 87-89, 125 | 通用 checksum helper；自身不提供独立物理断言 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/laser_acceleration/analysis_openpmd_rz.py` | laser injection / LPI | 87-89, 125 | 检查 RZ openPMD diagnostics 的 mesh shape、species ordering 和 `rho_<species>` 物理中心位置；重点在 diagnostics 合同，不在 laser 包络 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/laser_acceleration/analysis_refined_injection.py` | laser injection / LPI | 87-89, 125 | 检查 `refine_plasma=1` 时的总粒子数和 refinement edge 前方 `rho` 均匀性；重点在 AMR 注入一致性 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/laser_acceleration/inputs_base_1d` | laser-wakefield acceleration / moving-window skeleton | 87-89, 114-116, 125 | 1D LWFA 最小骨架：PEC 边界、moving window、连续电子注入、Gaussian laser antenna、FieldProbe reduced diagnostic；当前无独立 analysis，主要作为应用级 checksum/workflow 基线 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/laser_acceleration/inputs_base_2d` | laser-wakefield acceleration / moving-window skeleton | 71-76, 87-89, 114-116, 125 | 2D LWFA 骨架：PML、moving window、level-1 refined patch、连续背景电子和高斯 `beam`，同时写 Full diagnostics 与 moving-window `FieldProbe`；下游变体主要在这条骨架上切 boosted/MR/runtime path |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/laser_acceleration/inputs_base_3d` | laser-wakefield acceleration / moving-window skeleton | 87-89, 96, 114-116, 125 | 3D LWFA 骨架：周期横向 + 纵向 PEC、moving window、连续电子注入、openPMD Full diagnostics，以及 `regionofinterest/initialenergy` 粒子属性；当前主要作为 3D native/PICMI/Python/single-precision-comms 变体的 checksum 基线 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/laser_acceleration/inputs_base_rz` | laser-wakefield acceleration / moving-window skeleton / RZ | 87-89, 96, 114-116, 125 | RZ LWFA 骨架：`n_rz_azimuthal_modes=2`、moving window、连续背景电子、Gaussian `beam`、两种 species 变量输出；当前既服务 plain checksum 变体，也服务 `analysis_openpmd_rz.py` 的 diagnostics 合同 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/laser_acceleration/inputs_test_1d_laser_acceleration` | laser injection / LPI | 87-89, 125 | 1D LWFA/LPI 场景；当前 CMake 中无独立 analysis，主要依赖 checksum |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/laser_acceleration/inputs_test_1d_laser_acceleration_fluid_boosted` | fluid model | 101-104 | 1D boosted fluid WFA 基准；对应 `analysis_1d_fluid_boosted.py` 的理论对照 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/laser_acceleration/inputs_test_1d_laser_acceleration_picmi.py` | laser injection / LPI | 87-89, 125 | PICMI 版 1D LWFA 场景；当前主要依赖 checksum |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/laser_acceleration/inputs_test_2d_laser_acceleration_boosted` | laser injection / LPI | 87-89, 125 | 2D boosted LWFA 场景；moving window、plasma continuous injection 与 laser antenna 并存，当前主要依赖 checksum |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/laser_acceleration/inputs_test_2d_laser_acceleration_mr` | mesh refinement | 71-76 | 2D mesh-refinement LWFA 场景；当前主要依赖 checksum |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/laser_acceleration/inputs_test_2d_laser_acceleration_mr_picmi.py` | mesh refinement | 71-76 | PICMI 版 2D MR LWFA；当前主要依赖 checksum |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/laser_acceleration/inputs_test_2d_refined_injection` | laser injection / LPI | 87-89, 125 | 专门验证 `warpx.refine_plasma=1` 的 refined injection 场景；对应 `analysis_refined_injection.py` |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/laser_acceleration/inputs_test_3d_laser_acceleration` | laser injection / LPI | 87-89, 125 | 3D LWFA 场景；当前无独立 analysis，主要依赖 checksum |

| `Examples/Physics_applications/laser_acceleration/inputs_test_3d_laser_acceleration_python.py` | laser injection / LPI | 87-89, 125 | Python callback / pyWarpX 工作流变体；主要验证 afterstep callback 能访问粒子与场，再配合 checksum |

| `Examples/Physics_applications/laser_acceleration/plot_3d.py` | laser-wakefield acceleration / visualization helper | 87-89, 125 | `yt.SlicePlot` 可视化 helper；只展示 `Ey` 与 `rho` 的 2-panel slice，不构成 regression 断言，也不验证 wake amplitude 或 laser envelope 标度 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/laser_ion/analysis_default_regression.py` | laser injection / LPI | 87-89, 125 | checksum helper；作为应用场景结果基线，不直接断言离子截止能量等高层物理量 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/laser_ion/analysis_histogram_2D.py` | laser injection / LPI | 87-89, 125 | reduced diagnostic 可视化脚本；展示 `ParticleHistogram2D` 输出格式与轴信息，不构成 regression 断言 |

| `Examples/Physics_applications/laser_ion/inputs_test_2d_laser_ion_acc` | laser injection / LPI | 87-89, 125 | 2D 激光打靶场景；Gaussian laser + solid-density target + full/time-averaged/reduced diagnostics 组合样板 |

| `Examples/Physics_applications/pierce_diode/analysis_pierce_diode.py` | electrostatic / Child-Langmuir / diode | 105, 125 | 读取 openPMD `phi/Ez/rho/jz` 与离子 `z,uz`，把势分布和电流密度与 Child-Langmuir 理论解对照，并要求 `phi` 与 `J_z` 的相对误差都低于 `20%` |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/pierce_diode/inputs_test_1d_pierce_diode` | electrostatic / Child-Langmuir / diode | 105, 125 | 1D electrostatic Pierce diode；`boundary.potential_lo_z/hi_z` 固定两平行板势差，`ions.flux = J_CL/q_e` 直接把注入通量设到 Child-Langmuir 极限，用于检验空间电荷限制电流解 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/pierce_diode/plot_sim.py` | electrostatic / Child-Langmuir / diode | 105, 125 | 可视化脚本；复现 README 中的 `u_z/E_z/J_z/phi` 四幅图，不构成 regression 断言 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/plasma_acceleration/analysis_default_regression.py` | PWFA / boosted-frame application workflow | 88-89, 125 | 本地 checksum helper；自动识别 plotfile/openPMD 并调用 `evaluate_checksum(...)`，给 PWFA 应用骨架提供历史输出基线，不增加独立 wakefield 物理断言 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/plasma_acceleration/inputs_base_2d` | PWFA / moving window / mesh refinement | 71-76, 88-89, 125 | 2D 公共骨架：`CKC + PML + moving window + level-1 refined patch`，driver/beam Gaussian bunch 配合 `plasma_e` 的 `do_continuous_injection=1`；当前主要作为二维 PWFA workflow baseline 被下游 MR 与 boosted 变体复用 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/plasma_acceleration/inputs_base_3d` | PWFA / boosted frame / rigid bunch injection | 72, 88-89, 125 | 3D 公共骨架：`gamma_boost=10`、moving window、`particles.use_fdtd_nci_corr=1`、`driver/beam` rigid injection、`driverback` backward propagation、以及 `plasma_e/plasma_p` 的 density ramp；当前是 3D boosted PWFA 工作流主骨架 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/plasma_acceleration/inputs_test_1d_plasma_acceleration_picmi.py` | PWFA / PICMI minimal workflow | 88-89, 114-116, 125 | 1D PICMI 最小骨架：moving window、Dirichlet 场边界、absorbing 粒子边界、`esirkepov` 沉积、beam/plasma 双电子 species 与 field/particle diagnostics；当前无脚本内 assert，定位是前端 + workflow checksum baseline |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/plasma_acceleration/inputs_test_2d_plasma_acceleration_boosted` | PWFA / boosted frame / moving window | 72, 88-89, 125 | 2D boosted 变体：在二维 moving-window PWFA 骨架上打开 `gamma_boost=10`、rigid-injected `driver/beam` 与 `use_fdtd_nci_corr=1`；当前主要验证 boosted PWFA 运行链与 diagnostics 输出稳定性 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/plasma_acceleration/inputs_test_2d_plasma_acceleration_mr` | PWFA / mesh refinement | 71-76, 88-89, 125 | 2D MR 变体：直接复用 `inputs_base_2d`，重点是 level-1 refined patch 下的 moving-window PWFA 输出基线，而不是独立物理断言 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/plasma_acceleration/inputs_test_2d_plasma_acceleration_mr_momentum_conserving` | PWFA / mesh refinement / momentum-conserving gather | 71-76, 88-89, 125 | 2D MR + gather 变体：在 `inputs_base_2d` 上仅把 `algo.field_gathering` 切到 `momentum-conserving`，用于覆盖 refined PWFA 场景下的另一条 gather 路径 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/plasma_acceleration/inputs_test_3d_plasma_acceleration_boosted` | PWFA / boosted frame | 88-89, 125 | 3D boosted 最小基准：直接复用 `inputs_base_3d` 并把 `max_step` 缩到 `5`，主要覆盖 boosted PWFA 主骨架的短程稳定性与输出基线 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/plasma_acceleration/inputs_test_3d_plasma_acceleration_boosted_hybrid` | PWFA / boosted frame / hybrid grid | 53-56, 88-89, 125 | 3D boosted hybrid-grid 变体：在 `inputs_base_3d` 上切到 `warpx.grid_type = hybrid` 并关闭 `do_current_centering`，用于覆盖 boosted PWFA 在 hybrid-grid Maxwell 路径下的应用级基线 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/plasma_acceleration/inputs_test_3d_plasma_acceleration_mr_picmi.py` | PWFA / PICMI / mesh refinement scaffold | 71-76, 88-89, 114-116, 125 | 3D PICMI + MR 最小骨架：Python 脚本里显式 `add_refined_region(...)`、moving window、open/periodic mixed boundaries、beam/plasma `UniformDistribution` 与 field/particle diagnostics；当前无独立 assert，主要验证 PICMI refined-region 前端接线 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/plasma_acceleration/inputs_test_3d_plasma_acceleration_picmi.py` | PWFA / PICMI scaffold / non-boosted | 88-89, 114-116, 125 | 3D PICMI 最小骨架：moving window、periodic x/y + open z、beam/plasma `UniformDistribution` 与 field/particle diagnostics；WarpX README 明确标注它目前还没有跟原生 3D 例子一样启用 boosted frame，因此应诚实记录为非 boosted front-end scaffold |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/plasma_mirror/analysis_default_regression.py` | plasma mirror / laser-solid interaction | 125 | 本地 checksum helper；自动识别 plotfile/openPMD 并调用 `evaluate_checksum(...)`，为 2D plasma-mirror 场景提供历史输出基线，不增加独立反射率或高次谐波物理断言 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/plasma_mirror/inputs_test_2d_plasma_mirror` | plasma mirror / laser-solid interaction | 125 | 2D laser-solid surface-plasma 骨架：Gaussian laser 天线照射带 exponential-ramp + overdense plateau + rear exponential-ramp 的固体靶，配合 PML、三阶 shape factor、field filter 与 full diagnostics；当前是应用级 checksum baseline，不是解析 plasma-mirror benchmark |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/spacecraft_charging/analysis.py` | electrostatic / embedded boundary / spacecraft charging | 105, 110, 125 | 读取各步 `phi` 最小值并拟合 `phi(t)=v0(1-exp(-t/tau))`，要求拟合得到的浮动电位 `v0` 和充电时间常数 `tau` 分别落在 `4%` 与 `20%` 容差内 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/spacecraft_charging/analysis_default_regression.py` | electrostatic / embedded boundary / spacecraft charging | 105, 110, 125 | 通用 checksum helper；补充 spacecraft-charging 场景的历史输出基线，不替代 `v0/tau` 拟合断言 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/spacecraft_charging/inputs_test_rz_spacecraft_charging_picmi.py` | electrostatic / embedded boundary / spacecraft charging | 105, 110, 125 | RZ PICMI 导体球浸入热等离子体场景；同时使用 `ParticleBoundaryBufferWrapper` 在线累计 EB 收集电荷、`set_potential_on_eb(...)` 动态改写导体势、以及 `ParticleBoundaryScrapingDiagnostic(period=-1)` 末尾统一落盘 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/thomson_parabola_spectrometer/analysis.py` | Thomson parabola spectrometer / BoundaryScraping / test-particle optics | 22-26, 63-70, 110, 125 | 强分析：从 `screen/particles_at_zhi` 读取 detector hits，再用 `diag0` 的初始 `uz/id/mass` 恢复粒子初始能量，最终在 detector 平面重建按 species 与初始能量着色的 TPS 分离图；重点验证 `BoundaryScraping/openPMD` 与 prescribed-field ion optics 的联合合同 |
| `Examples/Physics_applications/thomson_parabola_spectrometer/analysis_default_regression.py` | Thomson parabola spectrometer / BoundaryScraping / test-particle optics | 22-26, 63-70, 110, 125 | 本地 checksum helper；自动识别 plotfile/openPMD 并调用 `evaluate_checksum(...)`，为 TPS 场景提供历史输出基线，不替代 `analysis.py` 的 detector-hit 重建 |

## Regression Checksum Benchmarks

| Benchmark | 初步主题 | 计划章节 | 验证用途 |
|---|---|---|---|
| `Langmuir_multi_2d_psatd_CC2_nodal.json` | Langmuir wave / plasma oscillation / PSATD / current correction | 9, 36-49, 124, 125 | checksum 基线；对应 2D nodal `PSATD + current_correction` 版本，analysis 额外复用 `analysis_2d.py` 比较解析 `Ex/Ez` 场解，并按 `analysis_utils.py` 强制检查 charge conservation |
| `Langmuir_multi_2d_psatd_QQ1_nodal.json` | Langmuir wave / plasma oscillation / PSATD / J-Rho coupling | 9, 36-49, 124, 125 | checksum 基线；对应 2D nodal `PSATD + JRhom_LL2` 版本，analysis 额外复用 `analysis_2d.py` 比较解析 `Ex/Ez` 场解 |
| `test_1d_background_mcc_picmi.json` | capacitive discharge / PIC-MCC / Turner benchmark | 92 | checksum 基线；对应 `inputs_base_1d_picmi.py --test --pythonsolver`，`analysis_1d.py` 额外把 `ion_density_case_1.npy` 与 Turner case-1 参考 profile 做 `allclose`，重点覆盖 PICMI MCC 接口与外部 Poisson solver callback |
